< Review>
-was pulled over at night by CHP on the 101. Multiple cars were going around same speed as me. Asked why he pulled me over and he said "your speed". Knew there was no point to argue with CHP officer. Signed citation and consulted Elizabeth afterwards. She patiently shared step-by-step instructions on what my alternatives were to dispute the officers erroneous accusation and offered strategy to get my bail money back and eliminating points in my record. We went thru the process and I was happily surprised when my citation was dismissed by the judge. Got back close to$500 in bail, got the points removed, and justice was served. The process was long and drawn out because courts move very slowly. Many insights on how the legal system operates was also shared.

If you felt you were unjustly treated by the police in a similar situation, I highly recommend reaching out and having a confidential discussion with Elizabeth on staff. Don't just accept and pay bail money to get it off your plate. It's the points that ultimately will affect your license and insurance premiums! You will be glad you did!< /Review>

<time>1493446369143< /time><Rating>5< /Rating><Review>I just moved to Oakland 10 months ago from Mumbai, India (yeah) so finding a waxing salon had been on my list for the first weeks. After reading all the reviews I gave it a try at this one. I booked my full body wax (full legs-arms-underarms and brazilian) online and was extremely relieved when they had an opening the very next day! WOOHOO!!! Giving that I haven't waxed since early June I was desperate and needed an immediate booking. I tried many other places but no one would book for a full body wax in such short notice. This place had a complimentary wax (bikini or underarm) for first timers so that was lovely. I went to the place on time and was greeted immediately by the receptionist who very fast brought up my booking appointment. Was immediately introduced to my waxer - Tigris who was lovely. The place was really clean and I was impressed. To all the ladies who have not given a 5 star I don't know what they expect more really. I have been waxing religiously since 2008 and have tried different type of waxing in many countries starting from local waxing in Everett, MA (terrible experience) to a luxurious SPA in Boston, MA to waxing in Albania (my hometown) with Australian wax products to Mumbai, India where I lived for 5 years before moving to Oakland. In my personal 8 years (and counting) of waxing experience, this place doesn't deserve less than 5 stars. Tigris was wonderful, she was nice and fun to talk to. She made me feel really comfortable and answered all my questions. This was for me the first experience having a full body wax with hard wax  - I usually have had soft wax applied for arms and legs and hard wax for only underarms and bikini area- but this was amazing and was done in less than 1.5 hours - YAY! The wax temperature was more than fine (I have been burned before in my past experiences) and Tigris was more than nice to ask me many times if the wax temperature was good for me. Also, very impressed with their techniques and products - pre waxing cleanser to remove oils, baby powder for the Brazilian area and pre wax oil for the wax to stick on hair and not skin and then waxing and after wards anti bumps/ingrown hair product and finally lotion - what more would anyone want for under 200$ for a full body wax? Sorry but if you still have complaints then something is wrong with you not the wax center. I will definitely return to this lovely place which is conveniently located 10min from my house and has time options to choose from. Clean, efficient, friendly and pain free. I came here on a cloudy Friday morning to grab breakfast. It‚Äôs atmosphere was welcoming and was greeted by a  friendly staff, a young dude. This review is solely based on customer service. About 2 weeks ago my friend gave me a 45 day pass for InShape. I was pretty excited to get to workout with my friend as many of those 45 days as we could push ourselves to do (I'm not really a gym person). So I went into InShape last week to claim the 45 day pass. I was attended by Jay, one of the sales associates I suppose. He was friendly and all but very persistent in getting me to sign up for a gym membership. After several attempts to refuse his offers, I finally gave in. I signed up for a three year membership at 34.99 a month, at least that's what I was told, for after I reviewed my paperwork, I noticed Jay had written 39.99. He also told me that I had ten days to cancel and that I would still get to keep my 45 days, which is all I wanted to begin with. So, nine days later I walk into the gym to cancel my membership. I hadn't even assisted to exercise all but one day. So there I am in the managers office. I told her I wanted to cancel my membership and get my 45 day pass, now a 36 day pass. Welp, I was denied the pass. Mr. Jay had the audacity to tell me, in front of his manager, that I had 5 days to cancel and still claim the 45 day pass. He basically lied to me in order to get me signed up. Why didn't he just validate the 45 day pass??? I probably would've only assisted half of those free days anyway (if that). The manager bitterly told me that she was going to cancel my account but that I could not keep the free pass, regardless of what Jay said because it violated company rules. She also told me that my account was going to be charged anyway and that I would later receive a refund. The problem here is that I wasn't going to have enough funds in my account to cover the cost. I really don't understand why these people couldn't just keep their word to begin with. Why did I have to deal with Mr. Jay's slip? In the end, isn't customer service about making your customer happy, so that they can potentially return to you or recommend your services to other people? Overall I think they need to reevaluate their customer service program. They need to get their act together and retrain their sales personnel. It is not fair for a customer to have to deal with the mistakes of their staff. This is the first review I've written on a business, in my life. This is how frustrating this situation has turned out to be to me. Grr, I even asked if there was another manager I could speak to. Blah, this concludes my review. I hope it helps.<//review>
